#First Choice (2000)
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100001001
	title = Japan_Demographic.100001001.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100001001.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Support for families
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001001.oA"
		set_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_CONSERVATIVES
		add_political_power = 50
		increase_social_spending = yes
		block_social_decrease = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_conservatives = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Talk up workers' rights
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001001.oB"
		set_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_PROGRESSIVES
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.02
		if = {
			limit = { has_economically_liberal_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_progressives = yes
			set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -5 }
			change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
			change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
			change_international_bankers_opinion = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Conservatives Demand More
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100001002
	title = Japan_Demographic.100001002.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100001002.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_small_shop

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_economically_liberal_government = yes
		has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_CONSERVATIVES
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_idea = fast_growth
				has_idea = economic_boom
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
		modifier = {
			has_stability < 0.5
			factor = 0.2
		}
		modifier = { # if economy stays healthy, stay off player's back
			has_idea = fast_growth
			factor = 3
		}
		modifier = { # if economy stays healthy, stay off player's back
			has_idea = economic_boom
			factor = 5
		}
	}

	#Accept
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001002.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001002.oA"
		set_temp_variable = { corp_change = -3 }
		modify_corporate_tax_rate_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
		change_international_bankers_opinion = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Stuff it!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001002.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001002.oB"
		add_political_power = -150
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -10 }
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
		change_international_bankers_opinion = yes
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.01 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Progressives Demand More
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100001003
	title = Japan_Demographic.100001003.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100001003.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_labor_protest

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_economically_liberal_government = yes
		has_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_APPEALED_PROGRESSIVES
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = JAP_protect_worker_rights
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
		modifier = {
			has_stability < 0.5
			factor = 0.6
		}
	}

	#No way!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001003.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001003.oA"
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_country_flag = JAP_DEMOGRAPHICS_CHAIN_REFUSED_PROGRESSIVES

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Accept union interests
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100001003.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100001003.oB"
		add_political_power = -300
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = industrial_conglomerates
				add_idea = labour_unions
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 7 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 15 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.02 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.02 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 21 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#First Depopulation Checkup Gate (2002)
#This is more gentle in consequences than the main sequence checkups
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100003200
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100003200.oA"
		if = { #You blew it!!
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_demographics_depopulation_reform < 1 }
			}
			JAP = { country_event = Japan_Demographic.100003201 }
		} else_if = { #Problems ahead!
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_demographics_depopulation_reform < 2 }
			}
			JAP = { country_event = Japan_Demographic.100003202 }
		} else = { #Doing great!
			JAP = { country_event = Japan_Demographic.100003203 }
		}
	}
}

#First Depopulation Checkup, No Problems
country_event = {
	id = Japan_Demographic.100003203
	title = Japan_Demographic.100003203.t
	desc = Japan_Demographic.100003203.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_prosperous_asakusa

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Great!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100003203.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100003203.oA"
		add_political_power = 50
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Extend our program!
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100003203.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100003203.oB"
		increase_social_spending = yes
		set_temp_variable = { corp_change = 2 }
		modify_corporate_tax_rate_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { pop_change = 2 }
		modify_population_tax_rate_effect = yes
		if = { #only if eco conservative
			limit = { has_economically_liberal_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_progressives = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	#Amend the budget
	option = {
		name = Japan_Demographic.100003203.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan_Demographic.100003203.oC"
		add_political_power = 100
		set_temp_variable = { corp_change = -3 }
		modify_corporate_tax_rate_effect = yes
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 50 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		if = { #only if not already conservative
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			steal_popularity_from_conservatives = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}
		activate_mission = JAP_demographic_main_reminder

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Replace Industrial Conglomerates with Labor Union?
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100001001
	title = Japan.100001001.t
	desc = Japan.100001001.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_labor_protest

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
		NOT = {
			has_idea = labour_unions
		}
	}

	#Better not
	option = {
		name = Japan.100001001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100001001.oA"
		add_political_power = 100

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Accept union interests
	option = {
		name = Japan.100001001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100001001.oB"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = industrial_conglomerates
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = industrial_conglomerates
				add_idea = labour_unions
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 10 }
		change_labour_unions_opinion = yes

	id = Japan.100002000
	title = Japan.100002000.t
	desc = Japan.100002000.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_yen

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #accept deal
		name = Japan.100002000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100002000.oA executed"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 30 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		FROM = {
			country_event = Japan.100002001
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 0.5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FROM.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = economic_mission
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = economic_mission
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #refuse deal
		name = Japan.100002000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100002000.oB executed"
		FROM = {
			country_event = Japan.100002002
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# NHK World chain
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100004010
	title = Japan.100004010.t
	desc = Japan.100004010.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_anchor_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Accept deal
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004010.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004010.oA executed"
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = Japan.100004010.t
			bonus = 1
			uses = 1
			category = CAT_internet_tech
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 0.5 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = FROM.id }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT.id }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					OR = { #only care to get a receipt from global if a major power or larger accepts
						has_idea = superpower
						has_idea = great_power
						has_idea = large_power
					}
					OR = { #if SEA, we want to know and potentially offer investments
						is_SE_Asia = yes
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				country_event = Japan.100004011
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Refuse deal
	option = {

		}

			limit = {
				has_tech_sharing_feature = yes

				category = CAT_industry
			}
		}

			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}

		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 5 }

		}

					target = FROM

				}
			}
		}
	}

				factor = 0.1

					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}

# Contribution to IHPCO
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100004141
	title = Japan.100004141.t
	desc = Japan.100004141.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_anchor_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Accept
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004141.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004141.oA executed"
		add_to_variable = {
			var = JAP.jap_ihcpo_funding_amt
			value = 1
		}
		FROM = { country_event = Japan.100004142 }
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_array = { FROM.jap_ihpco_members = ROOT.id }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Refuse
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004141.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004141.oB executed"
		add_political_power = 25
		FROM = { country_event = Japan.100004143 }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# More Funding
	option = {
		name = Japan.100004141.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100004141.oC executed"
		add_to_variable = {
			var = JAP.jap_ihcpo_funding_amt
			value = 2
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -30 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_to_array = { FROM.jap_ihpco_members = ROOT.id }
		FROM = { country_event = Japan.100004142 }

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Supercomputing Results Gate
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100004144
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100004144.oA"
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_ihcpo_funding_amt < 5 }
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.jap_ihpco_members
				country_event = { id = Japan.100004145 } # Supercomputing Bad Outcome
			}
		} else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_ihcpo_funding_amt < 8 }
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.jap_ihpco_members
				country_event = { id = Japan.100004146 } # Supercomputing Good Outcome
			}
		} else = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = JAP.jap_ihpco_members
				country_event = { id = Japan.100004147 } # Supercomputing Amazing Outcome
			}
		}
	}
}

		add_political_power = 50
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }

		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}

# Ground Forces: Next Generation Battle Tank
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100006101
	title = Japan.100006101.t
	desc = Japan.100006101.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Extend Type 90 Program
	option = {
		name = Japan.100006101.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100006101.oA executed"
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -20 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		# TODO: I have no idea if I did this right for non DLC so check it
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "No Step Back" }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = mbt_hull_1
				variant_name = "Type 90"
				amount = 50
				producer = JAP
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = Japan.100006101.t
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 5
				category = Cat_Computer_Systems
				category = Cat_Armour
				category = Cat_Armor_Engines
				category = Cat_Armor_Weapons
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = MBT_2
				amount = 100 # non DLC can't research components and refit so compensate them with more units
				producer = JAP
			}
		}

	}

	# Begin Type 10 Development
	option = {
		name = Japan.100006101.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100006101.oB executed"
		add_tech_bonus = { #TODO: should this be buffed?
			name = Japan.100006101.t
			bonus = 1
			ahead_reduction = 1
			uses = 1
			category = Cat_MBT
		}
	}
}

	}

	}

# Central Readiness Force
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009000
	title = Japan.100009000.t
	desc = Japan.100009000.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Implement Peacetime Readiness Force
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009000.oA executed"
		set_country_flag = JAP_ARTICLE_NINE_CENTRAL_READINESS_FORCE
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_army_manpower = { size < 100000 }
			}
			add_ideas = JAP_central_readiness_force
		}
		else = {
			#TODO: custom tooltip conditions for bonus not yet met
		}
		#TODO: custom tooltip bonus applied when manpower remains below 100,000
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}

	# Maintain Constant Readiness
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009000.oB executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = JAP_readiness_drills
			days = 365
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}
	}
}

#Unbreakable Chain: Decisive Victory Needed
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009200
	title = Japan.100009200.t
	desc = Japan.100009200.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# So Be It
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009200.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009200.oA executed"
		add_war_support = 0.10
		add_ideas = JAP_breakable
		#TODO: custom tooltip: idea will be removed if JAP capitulates!

		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
		}
	}

	# Offramp To Peace?
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009200.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009200.oB executed"
		white_peace = JAP
		set_truce = {
			target = JAP
			days = 365
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = Japan.100009201
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			clear_variable = jap_compelled_peace
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Unbreakable Chain: Peace Prevails!

	id = Japan.100009201
	title = Japan.100009201.t
	desc = Japan.100009201.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# What a relief!

		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
	}
}

#Unbreakable Chain: Quick Victory Slips Away!
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009202
	title = Japan.100009202.t
	desc = Japan.100009202.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Abandon the war
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009201.oA executed"
		white_peace = JAP
		set_truce = {
			target = JAP
			days = 730
		}
		add_political_power = -300
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.15 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = Japan.100009201
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			clear_variable = jap_compelled_peace
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}
	}

	# Victory is at hand!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009201.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009201.oB executed"
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.3
		}
		add_to_variable = { ROOT.jap_compelled_peace = 1 } # war support penalty increases each time, 10%, 20%, 30%
		set_temp_variable = { total_war_support_penalty = ROOT.jap_compelled_peace }
		multiply_temp_variable = { total_war_support_penalty = 0.1 }
		add_war_support = total_war_support_penalty
		add_political_power = -50
		activate_mission = JAP_dec_defense_compelled_peace

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

}

#Disputed Islands Mediation: Conference Setup
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009300
	title = Japan.100009300.t
	desc = Japan.100009300.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		add_to_array = {
			array = jap_mediation_conference_attendees
			value = JAP
		}
		add_to_array = { # riau
			array = jap_mediation_conference_states
			value = 627
		}
		add_to_array = { # natuna
			array = jap_mediation_conference_states
			value = 936
		}
		add_to_array = { # paracels
			array = jap_mediation_conference_states
			value = 813
		}
		add_to_array = { # scarborough shoal
			array = jap_mediation_conference_states
			value = 943
		}
		add_to_array = { # senkaku
			array = jap_mediation_conference_states
			value = 939
		}
		add_to_array = { # liancourt
			array = jap_mediation_conference_states
			value = 1099
		}
	}

	# Send Invitations
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009300.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009300.oA executed"
		country_event = {
			id = Japan.100009310 #conference gate
			days = 8
		}
		IND = { country_event = Japan.100009301 } #invitation to conference
		MAY = { country_event = Japan.100009301 } #invitation to conference
		VIE = { country_event = Japan.100009301 } #invitation to conference
		PHI = { country_event = Japan.100009301 } #invitation to conference
		KOR = { country_event = Japan.100009301 } #invitation to conference
		TAI = { country_event = Japan.100009301 } #invitation to conference
		CHI = { country_event = Japan.100009301 } #invitation to conference


		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	# Send Invitations, with "incentive" (guarantees AI attendance if player didn't befriend everyone)
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009300.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009300.oB executed"
		country_event = {
			id = Japan.100009310 #conference gate
			days = 8
		}
		increase_corruption = yes
		IND = { country_event = Japan.100009302 } #invitation to conference
		MAY = { country_event = Japan.100009302 } #invitation to conference
		VIE = { country_event = Japan.100009302 } #invitation to conference
		PHI = { country_event = Japan.100009302 } #invitation to conference
		KOR = { country_event = Japan.100009302 } #invitation to conference
		TAI = { country_event = Japan.100009302 } #invitation to conference
		CHI = { country_event = Japan.100009302 } #invitation to conference

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Disputed Islands Mediation: Invitation to Conference
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009301
	title = Japan.100009301.t
	desc = Japan.100009301.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Accept
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009301.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009301.oA executed"
		add_threat = -1.0
		JAP = {
			country_event = Japan.100009303 #accepts
			add_to_array = {
				array = jap_mediation_conference_attendees
				value = ROOT
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.1
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}

	# Decline
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009301.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009301.oB executed"
		add_political_power = 50
		add_war_support = 0.03
		JAP = {
			country_event = Japan.100009304 #declines
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = Japan.100009302.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Accept
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009302.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009302.oA executed"
		add_political_power = 200
		JAP = {
			country_event = Japan.100009303 #accepts
			add_to_array = {
				array = jap_mediation_conference_attendees
				value = ROOT
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	# Decline
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009302.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009302.oB executed"
		add_war_support = 0.05
		JAP = {
			country_event = Japan.100009304 #declines
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Disputed Islands Mediation: Conference Gate
#Gate, chooses the next event to serve until done
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009310
	title = Japan.100009310.t
	desc = Japan.100009310.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side0
		clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side1
		clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side2
		clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_favored_candidate
		clear_array = jap_mediation_conference_transfer_states
	}

	option = {
		name = Japan.100009310.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009310.oA executed"
		if = { # this event loop will proceed so long as there are unresolved disputes left (spratlys is a special case)
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_mediation_conference_states^num > 0 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { conference_target_state = jap_mediation_conference_states^0 }
			#add any states for this round to the transfer states array
			add_to_array = { jap_mediation_conference_transfer_states = conference_target_state }
			#set the sides for this round of negotiation
			var:conference_target_state = {
				owner = {
					set_temp_variable = { conference_side0 = THIS }
					every_other_country = { #we only want OTHER tags that have claims, not the owner
						limit = {
							var:conference_target_state = {
								OR = {
									is_claimed_by = PREV
									is_core_of = PREV
								}
							}
							is_in_array = {
								array = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_attendees
								value = THIS
							}
						}
						add_to_temp_array = { conference_current_claimants = THIS }
					}
				}
			}
			set_variable = { jap_mediation_conference_side0 = conference_side0 }
			#select the first two non-owner claimants and discard the rest to keep the list reasonable
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { conference_current_claimants^num > 1 }
				}
				set_variable = { jap_mediation_conference_side2 = conference_current_claimants^1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { conference_current_claimants^num > 0 }
				}
				set_variable = { jap_mediation_conference_side1 = conference_current_claimants^0 }
				# if we have at least one opposing side attending, we can attempt to resolve
				country_event = Japan.100009311 #Dispute Resolution Draft
			}
			else = {
				remove_from_array = { #pop the first element in the conference list so the next cycle knows what to do
					array = jap_mediation_conference_states
					index = 0
				}
				country_event = Japan.100009310 #Return to gate
			}
			remove_from_array = { #pop the first element in the conference list so the next cycle knows what to do
				array = jap_mediation_conference_states
				index = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { # spratlys not yet resolved

		}
		else = { # no more disputes - end conference

		}
	}
}

#Disputed Islands Mediation Main Sequence: Present Draft for <state name> Dispute Resolution (Japan)
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009311
	title = Japan.100009311.t
	desc = Japan.100009311.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Favor Side A
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009311.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009311.oA executed"
		set_variable = { jap_mediation_conference_favored_candidate = jap_mediation_conference_side0 }
		var:jap_mediation_conference_side0 = {
			add_political_power = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side1
			}
			var:jap_mediation_conference_side1 = {
				country_event = Japan.100009312 #loser compensation dialogue
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side2
			}
			var:jap_mediation_conference_side2 = {
				country_event = Japan.100009312 #loser compensation dialogue
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = Japan.100009310 #return to conference gate
			days = 1
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	# Favor Side B
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009311.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009311.oB executed"
		trigger = {
			has_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side1
		}
		set_variable = { jap_mediation_conference_favored_candidate = jap_mediation_conference_side1 }
		var:jap_mediation_conference_side1 = {
			add_political_power = 10
		}
		var:jap_mediation_conference_side0 = {
			country_event = Japan.100009312 #loser compensation dialogue
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side2
			}
			var:jap_mediation_conference_side2 = {
				country_event = Japan.100009312 #loser compensation dialogue
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = Japan.100009310 #return to conference gate
			days = 1
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	# Favor Side C
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009311.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009311.oC executed"
		trigger = {
			has_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side2
		}
		set_variable = { jap_mediation_conference_favored_candidate = jap_mediation_conference_side2 }
		var:jap_mediation_conference_side2 = {
			add_political_power = 10
		}
		var:jap_mediation_conference_side0 = {
			country_event = Japan.100009312 #loser compensation dialogue
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side1
			}
			var:jap_mediation_conference_side1 = {
				country_event = Japan.100009312 #loser compensation dialogue
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = Japan.100009310 #return to conference gate
			days = 1
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	# Favor Nobody
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009311.oD
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009311.oD executed"
		trigger = { #can't abstain from own conflict
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = jap_mediation_conference_side0
					original_tag = jap_mediation_conference_side1
					original_tag = jap_mediation_conference_side2
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { jap_mediation_conference_favored_candidate = -1 }
		country_event = {
			id = Japan.100009310 #return to conference gate
			days = 1
		}


		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Disputed Islands Mediation Main Sequence: Choose Compensation (Loser)
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009312
	title = Japan.100009312.t
	desc = Japan.100009312.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Financial Compensation
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009312.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009312.oA executed"
		set_variable = { ROOT.jap_mediation_conference_side_demand = 0 }
		var:JAP.jap_mediation_conference_favored_candidate = {
			country_event = Japan.100009313 # compensate FROM in exchange for dropped claim?
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
	# Dual Citizenship For Residents
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009312.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009312.oB executed"
		trigger = { #only makes sense if people from this tag actually live there
			var:JAP.jap_mediation_conference_transfer_states^0 = {
				state_population > 20000
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ROOT.jap_mediation_conference_side_demand = 1 }
		var:JAP.jap_mediation_conference_favored_candidate = {
			country_event = Japan.100009313 # compensate FROM in exchange for dropped claim?
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
	# 5 Year Favorable Trade Policy
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009312.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009312.oC executed"
		set_variable = { ROOT.jap_mediation_conference_side_demand = 2 }
		var:JAP.jap_mediation_conference_favored_candidate = {
			country_event = Japan.100009313 # compensate FROM in exchange for dropped claim?
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
	# Impossible
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009312.oD
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009312.oD executed"
		add_political_power = 50
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.05 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		add_war_support = 0.03

		var:JAP.jap_mediation_conference_favored_candidate = {
			country_event = Japan.100009314 # FROM refuse any deal to drop claim!
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Disputed Islands Mediation Main Sequence: Consider Compensation (Winner)
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009313
	title = Japan.100009313.t
	desc = Japan.100009313.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# We can accept this!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009313.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009313.oA executed"
		if = { # financial compensation
			limit = {
				check_variable = { FROM.jap_mediation_conference_side_demand = 0 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { transfer_cost = 10 }
			set_temp_variable = { transfer_state_population = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_transfer_states^0.state_population_k }
			multiply_temp_variable = { transfer_state_population = 0.1 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { transfer_cost = transfer_state_population }
			set_temp_variable = { transfer_state_buildings = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_transfer_states^0.num_of_factories }
			multiply_temp_variable = { transfer_state_buildings = 5 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { transfer_cost = transfer_state_buildings }

			FROM = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = transfer_cost }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
				var:JAP.jap_mediation_conference_transfer_states^0 = {
					if = { #clear the loser's claims and cores
						limit = {
							is_claimed_by = PREV
						}
						remove_claim_by = PREV
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = PREV
						}
						remove_core_of = PREV
					}
					if = { #if loser is the owner, transfer the state
						limit = {
							is_controlled_by = PREV
						}
						transfer_state_to = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { transfer_loss = transfer_cost }
			multiply_temp_variable = { transfer_loss = -1 }
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = transfer_loss }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		if = { # dual citizenship for residents
			limit = {
				check_variable = { FROM.jap_mediation_conference_side_demand = 1 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { transfer_state_population = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_transfer_states^0.state_population_k }
			multiply_temp_variable = { transfer_state_population = 0.5 }
			FROM = {
				capital_scope = {
					add_manpower = transfer_state_population #the citizens "exist" in two countries at once
				}
				var:JAP.jap_mediation_conference_transfer_states^0 = {
					if = { #clear the loser's claims and cores
						limit = {
							is_claimed_by = PREV
						}
						remove_claim_by = PREV
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = PREV
						}
						remove_core_of = PREV
					}
					if = { #if loser is the owner, transfer the state
						limit = {
							is_controlled_by = PREV
						}
						transfer_state_to = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = { # 5 year favorable trade policy #TODO: IT DOESNT WORK!!!! THE DECISION DOESNT AUTO ACTIVATE
			limit = {
				check_variable = { FROM.jap_mediation_conference_side_demand = 2 }
			}
			add_to_array = { jap_mediation_trade_policy_beneficiaries = FROM }
			FROM = {
				var:JAP.jap_mediation_conference_transfer_states^0 = {
					if = { #clear the loser's claims and cores
						limit = {
							is_claimed_by = PREV
						}
						remove_claim_by = PREV
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = PREV
						}
						remove_core_of = PREV
					}
					if = { #if loser is the owner, transfer the state
						limit = {
							is_controlled_by = PREV
						}
						transfer_state_to = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						original_tag = JAP
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = Japan.100009314 # TAG relinquishes claim
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = Japan.100009314 # TAG relinquishes claim
				days = 1
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
	# This is impossible!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009313.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009313.oB executed"
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						original_tag = JAP
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = Japan.100009315 # TAG refuses to relinquish
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = Japan.100009315 # TAG refuses to relinquish
				days = 1
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}

}

#Disputed Islands Mediation: <tag> Relinquishes Their Claim!
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009314
	title = Japan.100009314.t
	desc = Japan.100009314.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	# Wonderful!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100009314.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009314.oA executed"
		add_political_power = 50
		if = { # 5 year favorable trade policy
			limit = {
				check_variable = { jap_mediation_conference_side_demand = 2 }
			}
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = JAP_dec_mediation_benefits }
		}

		# clear variables and see if we are OK to go to the next stage in the conference
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_side0
			}
			JAP = {
				clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_side1
			}
			JAP = {
				clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_side2
			}
			JAP = {
				clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side2
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_side0
				}
				JAP = {
					clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side0
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_side1
				}
				JAP = {
					clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_side2
				}
				JAP = {
					clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side2
				}
			}
		}
		# I dont know if event effects in multiple countries create race conditions
		#so lets just shove it to another event in JAP
		JAP = {
			country_event = Japan.100009316 # conference end gate
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

			}

				clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side2
			}
		}
		FROM = {

				limit = {
					original_tag = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_side0
				}
				JAP = {
					clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side0
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_side1
				}
				JAP = {
					clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = JAP.jap_mediation_conference_side2
				}
				JAP = {
					clear_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side2
				}
			}
		}
		# I dont know if event effects in multiple countries create race conditions
		#so lets just shove it to another event in JAP

			country_event = Japan.100009316 # conference end gate
		}

			base = 10
		}

#Disputed Islands Mediation: End Gate
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100009316
	title = Japan.100009316.t
	desc = Japan.100009316.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = Japan.100009315.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: Japan.100009315.oA executed"
		JAP = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side0
						has_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side1
						has_variable = jap_mediation_conference_side2
					}
				}
				country_event = Japan.100009310 # conference gate
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}


#----------------------------------------------------------------
#Events Triggered by Date
#----------------------------------------------------------------
#[KATO] Start of Kato Rebellion Scenario
#Gate, when triggered chooses between an event or nothing, and sets one of two flags either way
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_EDT.120412001
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					}
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = mdmosjap_japan_kato.1
				set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_EXECUTED
			}
		} else = {
			JAP = { set_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_AVERTED }
		}
	}
}

#Battle of Amamioshima
#Gate, when triggered fires multiple events simultaneously
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_EDT.131222001
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NKO = {
			exists = yes
			has_country_leader = { name = "Kim Jong-il" }
		}
		JAP = {
			NOT = {
				OR = { # don't do this if the pyongyang conference has a chance to mend relations
					has_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_ONGOING
					has_country_flag = JAP_NKO_CONF_SUCCESS
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = JAP_AMAMIOSHIMA
	}

	option = {
		NKO = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222001 }
		JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan.131222002 }
	}

#[KATO]\"Ask people for\" Dissolution
#Gate, when triggered chooses between two events
country_event = {
	id = mdmosjap_EDT.170701001
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		JAP = {
			has_country_flag = MDMOSJAP_KATO_REBELLION_EPILOGUE_EARLY_ELECTION
		}
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
				}
			}
			JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan_kato.986 }
		} else = {
			JAP = { country_event = mdmosjap_japan_kato.987 }
		}
	}
}

#Direction of Foreign Policy
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100005000
	title = Japan.100005000.t
	desc = Japan.100005000.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Just SEA countries with democratic values
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005000.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005000.oA"
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_SE_Asia = yes
				NOT = {
					has_totalitarian_government = yes
					has_autocratic_government = yes
					has_idea = non_power
				}
			}
			country_event = Japan.100005001 # Japan Offers Developmental Assistance
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#All SEA countries, even limited democracies
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005000.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005000.oB"
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_SE_Asia = yes
				NOT = {
					has_idea = non_power
				}
			}
			country_event = Japan.100005001 # Japan Offers Developmental Assistance
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	#It should be spent at home!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005000.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005000.oC"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = JAP_domestic_development
			days = 365
		}
		add_political_power = 25

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}


#Japan Offers Developmental Assistance
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100005001
	title = Japan.100005001.t
	desc = Japan.100005001.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#We'll take it!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005001.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005001.oA"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = economic_mission
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = joint_infrastructure_projects
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = JAP }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = FROM }
		change_influence_percentage = yes

		set_country_flag = JAP_accepted_ODAC_assistance

		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = infrastructure
					size > 0
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = infrastructure
									size > 0
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = infrastructure
					size > 0
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = infrastructure
									size > 0
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		# Japan pays for it
		FROM = {
			country_event = Japan.100005002 # FROM accepts developmental assistance!
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}

	#Politely decline
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005001.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005001.oB"
		add_political_power = 50
		FROM = {
			country_event = Japan.100005003 # FROM declines developmental assistance
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	#Drag these colonizers through the mud!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005001.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005001.oC"
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = diplomatic_insults
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2.5 }
		change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes
		add_political_power = 50
		FROM = {
			country_event = Japan.100005004 # FROM aggressively denounces developmental assistance!
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Free Trade Area of the Asia-Pacific (China)
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100005010
	title = Japan.100005010.t
	desc = Japan.100005010.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Form (or expand) FTAAP
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005010.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005010.oA"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_liberal_government = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -200
		}
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 8 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_right = yes
		set_temp_variable = { jap_radical_change = 4 }
		jap_modify_radicalism_left = yes
		CHI = {
			country_event = Japan.100005020 # Enter FTAAP?
		}
		TAI = {
			country_event = Japan.100005020 # Enter FTAAP?
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Rather not
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005010.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005010.oB"
		add_political_power = 150
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_liberal_government = yes
				}
			}
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = { # all FTAAP offers finished and did not establish FTAAP
				has_completed_focus = JAP_china_relations
				has_completed_focus = JAP_south_korea_relations
				has_completed_focus = JAP_usa_relations
				has_completed_focus = JAP_sea_relations
				NOT = {
					has_idea = JAP_ftaap_member
				}
			}
			country_event = Japan.100005090 # Japan Turns Against Globalization!
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

#Japan Invites Us To FTAAP
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100005020
	title = Japan.100005020.t
	desc = Japan.100005020.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Join
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005020.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005020.oA"
		if = { # FTAAP does not exist yet
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = JAP_ftaap_member
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_array = { global.jap_ftaap_members = JAP }
			#dont add the idea here, let the monthly action do it
		}
		add_to_array = { global.jap_ftaap_members = ROOT }
		#dont add the idea here, let the monthly action do it
		# TODO: custom tooltip: the process will be formalized at the end of the month

		JAP = {
			country_event = Japan.100005021 # FROM enters the FTAAP!
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005020.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005020.oB"
		add_political_power = 50
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_liberal_government = yes
				}
			}
			set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
			set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		}

		JAP = {
			country_event = Japan.100005022 # FROM rejects free trade proposal!
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Japan Turns Against Globalization!
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100005090
	title = Japan.100005090.t
	desc = Japan.100005090.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Japan First!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005090.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005090.oA"
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = 20 }
		change_small_medium_business_owners_opinion = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_opinion = -10 }
		change_industrial_conglomerates_opinion = yes
		change_international_bankers_opinion = yes

		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 20 } #right wing populist
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Fair, Not Free Trade!
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005090.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005090.oB"
		add_political_power = 100
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 19 } #neutral communist
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		set_country_flag = JAP_FAIR_TRADE

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

	option = {
		name = Japan.100005200.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005200.oA"
		add_political_power = -50
		navy_experience = 25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_EDT.131222001 days = 14 random_days = 14 } # trigger Amami-Oshima naval event early
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Act is Defeated
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005200.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005200.oB"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_AMAMIOSHIMA
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.05
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}

	#Step Up Local Naval Patrols
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005200.oC
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005200.oC"
		trigger = { # only if the skirmish with NKO hasn't happened yet- otherwise why would there NOT be more naval patrols already?
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = JAP_AMAMIOSHIMA
			}
		}

		add_popularity = {
			ideology = nationalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		navy_experience = 15
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = mdmosjap_EDT.131222001 random_days = 7 } # trigger Amami-Oshima naval event early
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = Japan.100005201
	title = Japan.100005201.t
	desc = Japan.100005201.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Maintain Partnership
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005201.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005201.oA"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = nationalist
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 50
		}

		# add guarantee (visual only) if it has already vanished
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_guaranteed_by = USA
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				USA = {
					give_guarantee = JAP
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Insist on Equal Partnership
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005201.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005201.oB"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					jap_ruling_party_is_america_pro = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
		change_domestic_influence_percentage = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = -0.1
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = Japan.100005204.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005204.oA"
		give_guarantee = JAP

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Japan Is On Her Own
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005204.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005204.oB"
		clr_country_flag = JAP_GUARANTEE_FROM_USA
		if = {
			limit = {
				JAP = {
					jap_ruling_party_is_america_pro = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -150
		}
		set_country_flag = JAP_USA_BROKE_SECURITY_DEAL
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = left_alliance }
		JAP = {
			country_event = Japan.100005205 #USA Backs Away From Security Agreement
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}

}

#Japan Requests Final Decommission of Okinawa Bases (USA)
country_event = {
	id = Japan.100005210
	title = Japan.100005210.t
	desc = Japan.100005210.d
	picture = GFX_JAP_diet_address

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Begin the process
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005210.oA
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005210.oA"
		if = { # easier for public to accept if busy at home
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = usa_great_fiancial_crisis
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_political_power = -50
		} else = {
			add_political_power = -150
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = pro_american
		}

		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = Japan.100005211 hours = 12 random_hours = 24 } #USA Agrees To Hand Over Bases
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

	#Refuse
	option = {
		name = Japan.100005210.oB
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Japan.100005210.oB"
		add_political_power = 250
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.03 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.03 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = trespassing
		}

		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = Japan.100005212 hours = 12 random_hours = 24 } #USA Refuses To Hand Over Bases
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

		add_threat = 0.03

		ai_chance = {

		}
	}

			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.05 }
			add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			add_political_power = -50
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = japan_foreign_policy.288
	title = japan_foreign_policy.288.t
	desc = japan_foreign_policy.288.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_CAN_keystone_pipeline_building
	option = {
		name = japan_foreign_policy.288.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_foreign_policy.288.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value > 10
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = japan_foreign_policy.29 }
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 6 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = JAP }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = ROOT }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		random_owned_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = fossil_powerplant
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = oil
				amount = 2
			}
		}
		newline = yes
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -4.00 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = japan_foreign_policy.288.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: japan_foreign_policy.288.b executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_opinion = {
					target = JAP
					value < 10
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { country_event = japan_foreign_policy.30 }
	}
}
